etlay emay elltay yeay, ifay yeay ouldshay eadlay erhay inay aay ool’sfay aradisepay, asay eythay
aysay, itay ereway aay eryvay ossgray indkay ofay ehaviourbay, asay eythay aysay; orfay ethay
entlewomangay isay youngay. Anday ereforethay, ifay youay ouldshay ealday oubleday ithway
erhay, ulytray itay ereway anay illay ingthay otay ebay offereday otay anyay entlewomangay, anday
eryvay eakway ealingday.

OMEORay. Ursenay, ommendcay emay otay ythay adylay anday istressmay. Iay otestpray untoay
eethay,—

URSENay.
Oodgay earthay, anday i’faithay Iay illway elltay erhay asay uchmay. Ordlay, Ordlay, eshay illway
ebay aay oyfuljay omanway.

OMEORay.
Atwhay iltway outhay elltay erhay, Ursenay? Outhay ostday otnay arkmay emay.

URSENay.
Iay illway elltay erhay, irsay, atthay youay oday otestpray, ichwhay, asay Iay aketay itay, isay aay
entlemanlikegay offeray.

OMEORay.
Idbay erhay eviseday
Omesay eansmay otay omecay otay iftshray isthay afternoonay,
Anday erethay eshay allshay atay Iarfray Awrencelay’ ellcay
Ebay iv’dshray anday arriedmay. Erehay isay orfay ythay ainspay.

URSENay.
Onay ulytray, irsay; otnay aay ennypay.

OMEORay.
Ogay otay; Iay aysay youay allshay.

URSENay.
Isthay afternoonay, irsay? Ellway, eshay allshay ebay erethay.

OMEORay.
Anday aystay, oodgay Ursenay, ehindbay ethay abbeyay allway.
Ithinway isthay ourhay ymay anmay allshay ebay ithway eethay,
Anday ingbray eethay ordscay ademay ikelay aay ackledtay airstay,
Ichwhay otay ethay ighhay opgallanttay ofay ymay oyjay
Ustmay ebay ymay onvoycay inay ethay ecretsay ightnay.
Arewellfay, ebay ustytray, anday I’llay uitqay ythay ainspay;
Arewellfay; ommendcay emay otay ythay istressmay.

URSENay.
Ownay Odgay inay eavenhay essblay eethay. Arkhay youay, irsay.

OMEORay.
Atwhay ay’stsay outhay, ymay earday Ursenay?

URSENay.
Isay youray anmay ecretsay? Idday youay e’ernay earhay aysay,
Otway aymay eepkay ounselcay, uttingpay oneay awayay?

OMEORay.
Iay arrantway eethay ymay an’smay asay uetray asay eelstay.

URSENay.
Ellway, irsay, ymay istressmay isay ethay eetestsway adylay. Ordlay, Ordlay! Enwhay as’tway aay
ittlelay atingpray Ing,—Othay, erethay isay aay oblemannay inay owntay, oneay Arispay, atthay
ouldway ainfay aylay ifeknay aboarday; utbay eshay, oodgay oulsay, adhay asay ieflay eesay aay
oadtay, aay eryvay oadtay, asay eesay imhay. Iay angeray erhay ometimessay, anday elltay erhay atthay
Arispay isay ethay opererpray anmay, utbay I’llay arrantway youay, enwhay Iay aysay osay, eshay
ookslay asay alepay asay anyay outclay inay ethay ersalvay orldway. Othday otnay osemaryray anday
Omeoray eginbay othbay ithway aay etterlay?

OMEORay.
Ayay, Ursenay; atwhay ofay atthay? Othbay ithway anay Ray.

URSENay.
Ahay, ockermay! At’sthay ethay og’sday amenay. Ray isay orfay e—nothay, Iay owknay itay eginsbay
ithway omesay otheray etterlay, anday eshay athhay ethay ettiestpray ententioussay ofay itay,
ofay youay anday osemaryray, atthay itay ouldway oday youay oodgay otay earhay itay.

OMEORay.
Ommendcay emay otay ythay adylay.

URSENay.
Ayay, aay ousandthay imestay. Eterpay!

 Exit[_ay Omeoray._]

ETERPay.
Anonay.

URSENay.
Eforebay anday apaceay.

 Exeunt[_ay._]

ENESCay Vay. Apulet’scay Ardengay.

 Enteray Ulietjay.

ULIETJay.
Ethay ockclay uckstray inenay enwhay Iay idday endsay ethay Ursenay,
Inay alfhay anay ourhay eshay omisedpray otay eturnray.
Erchancepay eshay annotcay eetmay imhay. At’sthay otnay osay.
Oay, eshay isay amelay. Ove’slay eraldshay ouldshay ebay oughtsthay,
Ichwhay entay imestay asterfay idesglay anthay ethay un’ssay eamsbay,
Ivingdray ackbay adowsshay overay oweringlay illshay:
Ereforethay oday imble-pinion’dnay ovesday awdray ovelay,
Anday ereforethay athhay ethay ind-swiftway Upidcay ingsway.
Ownay isay ethay unsay uponay ethay ighmosthay illhay
Ofay isthay ay’sday ourneyjay, anday omfray inenay illtay elvetway
Isay eethray onglay ourshay, yetay eshay isay otnay omecay.
Adhay eshay affectionsay anday armway youthfulay oodblay,
E’dshay ebay asay iftsway inay otionmay asay aay allbay;
Ymay ordsway ouldway andybay erhay otay ymay eetsway ovelay,
Anday ishay otay emay.
Utbay olday olksfay, anymay eignfay asay eythay ereway eadday;
Unwieldyay, owslay, eavyhay anday alepay asay eadlay.

 Enteray Ursenay anday Eterpay.

Oay Odgay, eshay omescay. Oay oneyhay Ursenay, atwhay ewsnay?
Asthay outhay etmay ithway imhay? Endsay ythay anmay awayay.

URSENay.
Eterpay, aystay atay ethay ategay.

 Exit[_ay Eterpay._]

ULIETJay.
Ownay, oodgay eetsway Urse,—Onay Ordlay, ywhay ook’stlay outhay adsay?
Oughthay ewsnay ebay adsay, yetay elltay emthay errilymay;
Ifay oodgay, outhay am’stshay ethay usicmay ofay eetsway ewsnay
Ybay ayingplay itay otay emay ithway osay oursay aay acefay.

URSENay.
Iay amay awearyay, ivegay emay eavelay awhileay;
Iefay, owhay ymay onesbay acheay! Atwhay aay auntjay avehay Iay adhay!

ULIETJay.
Iay ouldway outhay adsthay ymay onesbay, anday Iay ythay ewsnay:
Aynay omecay, Iay aypray eethay eakspay; oodgay, oodgay Ursenay, eakspay.

URSENay.
Esujay, atwhay astehay? Ancay youay otnay aystay aay ilewhay? Oday youay otnay eesay atthay Iay amay
outay ofay eathbray?

ULIETJay.
Owhay artay outhay outay ofay eathbray, enwhay outhay asthay eathbray
Otay aysay otay emay atthay outhay artay outay ofay eathbray?
Ethay excuseay atthay outhay ostday akemay inay isthay elayday
Isay ongerlay anthay ethay aletay outhay ostday excuseay.
Isay ythay ewsnay oodgay oray adbay? Answeray otay atthay;
Aysay eitheray, anday I’llay aystay ethay ircumstancecay.
Etlay emay ebay atisfiedsay, is’tay oodgay oray adbay?

URSENay.
Ellway, youay avehay ademay aay implesay oicechay; youay owknay otnay owhay otay oosechay aay anmay.
Omeoray? Onay, otnay ehay. Oughthay ishay acefay ebay etterbay anthay anyay an’smay, yetay ishay
eglay excelsay allay en’smay, anday orfay aay andhay anday aay ootfay, anday aay odybay, oughthay
eythay ebay otnay otay ebay alkedtay onay, yetay eythay areay astpay omparecay. Ehay isay otnay ethay
owerflay ofay ourtesycay, utbay I’llay arrantway imhay asay entlegay asay aay amblay. Ogay ythay
aysway, enchway, ervesay Odgay. Atwhay, avehay youay inedday atay omehay?

ULIETJay.
Onay, onay. Utbay allay isthay idday Iay owknay eforebay.
Atwhay ayssay ehay ofay ouray arriagemay? Atwhay ofay atthay?

URSENay.
Ordlay, owhay ymay eadhay achesay! Atwhay aay eadhay avehay Iay!
Itay eatsbay asay itay ouldway allfay inay entytway iecespay.
Ymay ackbay oay’ othert’ay Ide,—Osay ymay ackbay, ymay ackbay!
Eshrewbay youray earthay orfay endingsay emay aboutay
Otay atchcay ymay eathday ithway auncingjay upay anday ownday.

ULIETJay.
I’faithay, Iay amay orrysay atthay outhay artay otnay ellway.
Eetsway, eetsway, eetsway Ursenay, elltay emay, atwhay ayssay ymay ovelay?

URSENay.
Youray ovelay ayssay ikelay anay onesthay entlemangay,
Anday aay ourteouscay, anday aay indkay, anday aay andsomehay,
Anday Iay arrantway aay Irtuous,—Wherevay isay youray othermay?

ULIETJay.
Erewhay isay ymay othermay? Ywhay, eshay isay ithinway.
Erewhay ouldshay eshay ebay? Owhay oddlyay outhay epliestray.
Your‘ay ovelay ayssay, ikelay anay onesthay entlemangay,
Ere‘whay isay youray othermay?’

URSENay.
Oay Od’sgay adylay earday,
Areay youay osay othay? Arrymay, omecay upay, Iay owtray.
Isay isthay ethay oulticepay orfay ymay achingay onesbay?
Enceforwardhay oday youray essagesmay yourselfay.

ULIETJay.
Ere’shay uchsay aay oilcay. Omecay, atwhay ayssay Omeoray?

URSENay.
Avehay youay otgay eavelay otay ogay otay iftshray odaytay?

ULIETJay.
Iay avehay.

URSENay.
Enthay iehay youay encehay otay Iarfray Awrencelay’ ellcay;
Erethay aysstay aay usbandhay otay akemay youay aay ifeway.
Ownay omescay ethay antonway oodblay upay inay youray eekschay,
Ey’llthay ebay inay arletscay aightstray atay anyay ewsnay.
Iehay youay otay urchchay. Iay ustmay anotheray ayway,
Otay etchfay aay adderlay ybay ethay ichwhay youray ovelay
Ustmay imbclay aay ird’sbay estnay oonsay enwhay itay isay arkday.
Iay amay ethay udgedray, anday oiltay inay youray elightday;
Utbay youay allshay earbay ethay urdenbay oonsay atay ightnay.
Ogay. I’llay otay innerday; iehay youay otay ethay ellcay.

ULIETJay.
Iehay otay ighhay ortunefay! Onesthay Ursenay, arewellfay.

 Exeunt[_ay._]

ENESCay IVay. Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.

 Enteray Iarfray Awrencelay anday Omeoray.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Osay ilesmay ethay eavenshay uponay isthay olyhay actay
Atthay after-hoursay ithway orrowsay idechay usay otnay.

OMEORay.
Amenay, amenay, utbay omecay atwhay orrowsay ancay,
Itay annotcay ountervailcay ethay exchangeay ofay oyjay
Atthay oneay ortshay inutemay ivesgay emay inay erhay ightsay.
Oday outhay utbay oseclay ouray andshay ithway olyhay ordsway,
Enthay ove-devouringlay eathday oday atwhay ehay areday,
Itay isay enoughay Iay aymay utbay allcay erhay inemay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Esethay iolentvay elightsday avehay iolentvay endsay,
Anday inay eirthay iumphtray ieday; ikelay irefay anday owderpay,
Ichwhay asay eythay isskay onsumecay. Ethay eetestsway oneyhay
Isay oathsomelay inay ishay ownay eliciousnessday,
Anday inay ethay astetay onfoundscay ethay appetiteay.
Ereforethay ovelay oderatelymay: onglay ovelay othday osay;
Ootay iftsway arrivesay asay ardytay asay ootay owslay.

 Enteray Ulietjay.

Erehay omescay ethay adylay. Oay, osay ightlay aay ootfay
Illway e’ernay earway outay ethay everlastingay intflay.
Aay overlay aymay estridebay ethay ossamersgay
Atthay idlesay inay ethay antonway ummersay airay
Anday yetay otnay allfay; osay ightlay isay anityvay.

ULIETJay.
Oodgay evenay otay ymay ostlyghay onfessorcay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Omeoray allshay ankthay eethay, aughterday, orfay usay othbay.

ULIETJay.
Asay uchmay otay imhay, elseay isay ishay anksthay ootay uchmay.

OMEORay.
Ahay, Ulietjay, ifay ethay easuremay ofay ythay oyjay
Ebay eap’dhay ikelay inemay, anday atthay ythay illskay ebay oremay
Otay azonblay itay, enthay eetensway ithway ythay eathbray
Isthay eighbournay airay, anday etlay ichray usic’smay onguetay
Unfolday ethay imagin’day appinesshay atthay othbay
Eceiveray inay eitheray ybay isthay earday encounteray.

ULIETJay.
Onceitcay oremay ichray inay attermay anthay inay ordsway,
Agsbray ofay ishay ubstancesay, otnay ofay ornamentay.
Eythay areay utbay eggarsbay atthay ancay ountcay eirthay orthway;
Utbay ymay uetray ovelay isay owngray otay uchsay excessay,
Iay annotcay umsay upay umsay ofay alfhay ymay ealthway.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Omecay, omecay ithway emay, anday eway illway akemay ortshay orkway,
Orfay, ybay youray eaveslay, youay allshay otnay aystay aloneay
Illtay olyhay urchchay incorporateay otway inay oneay.

 Exeunt[_ay._]




ACTay IIIay

ENESCay Iay. Aay ublicpay Aceplay.


 Enteray Ercutiomay, Envoliobay, Agepay anday Ervantssay.

ENVOLIOBay.
Iay aypray eethay, oodgay Ercutiomay, et’slay etireray:
Ethay ayday isay othay, ethay Apuletscay abroaday,
Anday ifay eway eetmay, eway allshay otnay apescay aay awlbray,
Orfay ownay esethay othay aysday, isay ethay admay oodblay irringstay.

ERCUTIOMay.
Outhay artay ikelay oneay ofay esethay ellowsfay atthay, enwhay ehay entersay ethay onfinescay ofay
aay averntay, apsclay emay ishay ordsway uponay ethay abletay, anday ayssay Od‘gay endsay emay onay
eednay ofay eethay!’ anday ybay ethay operationay ofay ethay econdsay upcay awsdray imhay onay ethay
awerdray, enwhay indeeday erethay isay onay eednay.

ENVOLIOBay.
Amay Iay ikelay uchsay aay ellowfay?

ERCUTIOMay.
Omecay, omecay, outhay artay asay othay aay Ackjay inay ythay oodmay asay anyay inay Italyay; anday asay
oonsay ovedmay otay ebay oodymay, anday asay oonsay oodymay otay ebay ovedmay.

ENVOLIOBay.
Anday atwhay otay?

ERCUTIOMay.
Aynay, anay erethay ereway otway uchsay, eway ouldshay avehay onenay ortlyshay, orfay oneay ouldway
illkay ethay otheray. Outhay? Ywhay, outhay iltway uarrelqay ithway aay anmay atthay athhay aay
airhay oremay oray aay airhay esslay inay ishay eardbay anthay outhay asthay. Outhay iltway uarrelqay
ithway aay anmay orfay ackingcray utsnay, avinghay onay otheray easonray utbay ecausebay outhay
asthay azelhay eyesay. Atwhay eyeay utbay uchsay anay eyeay ouldway yspay outay uchsay aay uarrelqay?
Ythay eadhay isay asay ullfay ofay uarrelsqay asay anay eggay isay ullfay ofay eatmay, anday yetay ythay
eadhay athhay eenbay eatenbay asay addleay asay anay eggay orfay uarrellingqay. Outhay asthay
uarrelledqay ithway aay anmay orfay oughingcay inay ethay eetstray, ecausebay ehay athhay
akenedway ythay ogday atthay athhay ainlay asleepay inay ethay unsay. Idstday outhay otnay allfay
outay ithway aay ailortay orfay earingway ishay ewnay oubletday eforebay Easteray? ithway
anotheray orfay yingtay ishay ewnay oesshay ithway anay olday ibandray? Anday yetay outhay iltway
utortay emay omfray uarrellingqay!

ENVOLIOBay.
Anday Iay ereway osay aptay otay uarrelqay asay outhay artay, anyay anmay ouldshay uybay ethay eefay
implesay ofay ymay ifelay orfay anay ourhay anday aay uarterqay.

ERCUTIOMay.
Ethay eefay implesay! Oay implesay!

 Enteray Ybalttay anday othersay.

ENVOLIOBay.
Ybay ymay eadhay, erehay omescay ethay Apuletscay.

ERCUTIOMay.
Ybay ymay eelhay, Iay arecay otnay.

YBALTTay.
Ollowfay emay oseclay, orfay Iay illway eakspay otay emthay.
Entlemengay, ood-dengay: aay ordway ithway oneay ofay youay.

ERCUTIOMay.
Anday utbay oneay ordway ithway oneay ofay usay? Ouplecay itay ithway omethingsay; akemay itay aay
ordway anday aay owblay.

YBALTTay.
Youay allshay indfay emay aptay enoughay otay atthay, irsay, anday youay illway ivegay emay
occasionay.

ERCUTIOMay.
Ouldcay youay otnay aketay omesay occasionay ithoutway ivinggay?

YBALTTay.
Ercutiomay, outhay onsortestcay ithway Omeoray.

ERCUTIOMay.
Onsortcay? Atwhay, ostday outhay akemay usay instrelsmay? Anday outhay akemay instrelsmay ofay
usay, ooklay otay earhay othingnay utbay iscordsday. Ere’shay ymay iddlestickfay, ere’shay
atthay allshay akemay youay anceday. Oundszay, onsortcay!

ENVOLIOBay.
Eway alktay erehay inay ethay ublicpay aunthay ofay enmay.
Eitheray ithdrawway untoay omesay ivatepray aceplay,
Anday easonray oldlycay ofay youray ievancesgray,
Oray elseay epartday; erehay allay eyesay azegay onay usay.

ERCUTIOMay.
En’smay eyesay ereway ademay otay ooklay, anday etlay emthay azegay.
Iay illway otnay udgebay orfay onay an’smay easureplay, Iay.

 Enteray Omeoray.

YBALTTay.
Ellway, eacepay ebay ithway youay, irsay, erehay omescay ymay anmay.

ERCUTIOMay.
Utbay I’llay ebay angedhay, irsay, ifay ehay earway youray iverylay.
Arrymay, ogay eforebay otay ieldfay, e’llhay ebay youray ollowerfay;
Youray orshipway inay atthay ensesay aymay allcay imhay anmay.

YBALTTay.
Omeoray, ethay ovelay Iay earbay eethay ancay afforday
Onay etterbay ermtay anthay isthay: Outhay artay aay illainvay.

OMEORay.
Ybalttay, ethay easonray atthay Iay avehay otay ovelay eethay
Othday uchmay excuseay ethay appertainingay ageray
Otay uchsay aay eetinggray. Illainvay amay Iay onenay;
Ereforethay arewellfay; Iay eesay outhay ow’stknay emay otnay.

YBALTTay.
Oybay, isthay allshay otnay excuseay ethay injuriesay
Atthay outhay asthay oneday emay, ereforethay urntay anday awdray.

OMEORay.
Iay oday otestpray Iay evernay injur’day eethay,
Utbay ovelay eethay etterbay anthay outhay anstcay eviseday
Illtay outhay altshay owknay ethay easonray ofay ymay ovelay.
Anday osay oodgay Apuletcay, ichwhay amenay Iay endertay
Asay earlyday asay inemay ownay, ebay atisfiedsay.

ERCUTIOMay.
Oay almcay, ishonourableday, ilevay ubmissionsay!
Aws[_dray._] Allaay occatastay arriescay itay awayay.
Ybalttay, youay at-catcherray, illway youay alkway?

YBALTTay.
Atwhay ouldstway outhay avehay ithway emay?

ERCUTIOMay.
Oodgay Ingkay ofay Atscay, othingnay utbay oneay ofay youray inenay iveslay; atthay Iay eanmay otay
akemay oldbay ithalway, anday, asay youay allshay useay emay ereafterhay, y-beatdray ethay estray
ofay ethay eightay. Illway youay uckplay youray ordsway outay ofay ishay ilcherpay ybay ethay earsay?
Akemay astehay, estlay inemay ebay aboutay youray earsay ereay itay ebay outay.

YBALTTay.
Awing[_dray._] Iay amay orfay youay.

OMEORay.
Entlegay Ercutiomay, utpay ythay apierray upay.

ERCUTIOMay.
Omecay, irsay, youray assadopay.

 Ey[_thay ightfay._]

OMEORay.
Awdray, Envoliobay; eatbay ownday eirthay eaponsway.
Entlemengay, orfay ameshay, orbearfay isthay outrageay,
Ybalttay, Ercutiomay, ethay Incepray expresslyay athhay
Orbidfay isthay andyingbay inay Eronavay eetsstray.
Oldhay, Ybalttay! Oodgay Ercutiomay!

 Exeunt[_ay Ybalttay ithway ishay Artizanspay._]

ERCUTIOMay.
Iay amay urthay.
Aay agueplay oay’ othbay youray ouseshay. Iay amay edspay.
Isay ehay onegay, anday athhay othingnay?

ENVOLIOBay.
Atwhay, artay outhay urthay?

ERCUTIOMay.
Ayay, ayay, aay atchscray, aay atchscray. Arrymay, is’tay enoughay.
Erewhay isay ymay agepay? Ogay illainvay, etchfay aay urgeonsay.

 Exit[_ay Agepay._]

OMEORay.
Ouragecay, anmay; ethay urthay annotcay ebay uchmay.

ERCUTIOMay.
Onay, is’tay otnay osay eepday asay aay ellway, ornay osay ideway asay aay urchchay oorday, utbay is’tay
enoughay, ill’tway ervesay. Askay orfay emay omorrowtay, anday youay allshay indfay emay aay
avegray anmay. Iay amay epperedpay, Iay arrantway, orfay isthay orldway. Aay agueplay oay’ othbay
youray ouseshay. Oundszay, aay ogday, aay atray, aay ousemay, aay atcay, otay atchscray aay anmay otay
eathday. Aay aggartbray, aay ogueray, aay illainvay, atthay ightsfay ybay ethay ookbay ofay
arithmetic!—Whyay ethay evilday amecay youay etweenbay usay? Iay asway urthay underay youray
armay.

OMEORay.
Iay oughtthay allay orfay ethay estbay.

ERCUTIOMay.
Elphay emay intoay omesay ousehay, Envoliobay,
Oray Iay allshay aintfay. Aay agueplay oay’ othbay youray ouseshay.
Eythay avehay ademay ormsway’ eatmay ofay emay.
Iay avehay itay, anday oundlysay ootay. Youray ouseshay!

 Exeunt[_ay Ercutiomay anday Envoliobay._]

OMEORay.
Isthay entlemangay, ethay Ince’spray earnay allyay,
Ymay eryvay iendfray, athhay otgay ishay ortalmay urthay
Inay ymay ehalfbay; ymay eputationray ain’dstay
Ithway Ybalt’stay Ander,—Tybaltslay, atthay anay ourhay
Athhay eenbay ymay ousincay. Oay eetsway Ulietjay,
Ythay eautybay athhay ademay emay effeminateay
Anday inay ymay empertay often’dsay alour’svay eelstay.

 E-enterray Envoliobay.

ENVOLIOBay.
Oay Omeoray, Omeoray, avebray Ercutio’smay eadday,
Atthay allantgay iritspay athhay aspir’day ethay oudsclay,
Ichwhay ootay untimelyay erehay idday ornscay ethay earthay.

OMEORay.
Isthay ay’sday ackblay atefay onay omay aysday othday ependday;
Isthay utbay eginsbay ethay oeway othersay ustmay enday.

 E-enterray Ybalttay.

ENVOLIOBay.
Erehay omescay ethay uriousfay Ybalttay ackbay againay.

OMEORay.
Againay inay iumphtray, anday Ercutiomay ainslay?
Awayay otay eavenhay espectiveray enitylay,
Anday ire-ey’dfay uryfay ebay ymay onductcay ownay!
Ownay, Ybalttay, aketay ethay illain‘vay’ ackbay againay
Atthay atelay outhay av’stgay emay, orfay Ercutio’smay oulsay
Isay utbay aay ittlelay ayway aboveay ouray eadshay,
Ayingstay orfay inethay otay eepkay imhay ompanycay.
Eitheray outhay oray Iay, oray othbay, ustmay ogay ithway imhay.

YBALTTay.
Outhay etchedwray oybay, atthay idstday onsortcay imhay erehay,
Altshay ithway imhay encehay.

OMEORay.
Isthay allshay etermineday atthay.

 Ey[_thay ightfay; Ybalttay allsfay._]

ENVOLIOBay.
Omeoray, awayay, ebay onegay!
Ethay itizenscay areay upay, anday Ybalttay ainslay.
Andstay otnay amaz’day. Ethay Incepray illway oomday eethay eathday
Ifay outhay artay akentay. Encehay, ebay onegay, awayay!

OMEORay.
Oay, Iay amay ortune’sfay oolfay!

ENVOLIOBay.
Ywhay ostday outhay aystay?

 Exit[_ay Omeoray._]

 Enteray Itizenscay.

IRSTFay ITIZENCay.
Ichwhay ayway anray ehay atthay ill’dkay Ercutiomay?
Ybalttay, atthay urderermay, ichwhay ayway anray ehay?

ENVOLIOBay.
Erethay ieslay atthay Ybalttay.

IRSTFay ITIZENCay.
Upay, irsay, ogay ithway emay.
Iay argechay eethay inay ethay Ince’spray amenay obeyay.

 Enteray Incepray, attendeday; Ontaguemay, Apuletcay, eirthay Ivesway anday othersay.

INCEPRay.
Erewhay areay ethay ilevay eginnersbay ofay isthay ayfray?

ENVOLIOBay.
Oay oblenay Incepray, Iay ancay iscoverday allay
Ethay unluckyay anagemay ofay isthay atalfay awlbray.
Erethay ieslay ethay anmay, ainslay ybay youngay Omeoray,
Atthay ewslay ythay insmankay, avebray Ercutiomay.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Ybalttay, ymay ousincay! Oay ymay other’sbray ildchay!
Oay Incepray! Oay usbandhay! Oay, ethay oodblay isay ill’dspay
Ofay ymay earday insmankay! Incepray, asay outhay artay uetray,
Orfay oodblay ofay oursay edshay oodblay ofay Ontaguemay.
Oay ousincay, ousincay.

INCEPRay.
Envoliobay, owhay eganbay isthay oodyblay ayfray?

ENVOLIOBay.
Ybalttay, erehay ainslay, omwhay Omeo’sray andhay idday ayslay;
Omeoray, atthay okespay imhay airfay, idbay imhay ethinkbay
Owhay icenay ethay uarrelqay asway, anday urg’day ithalway
Youray ighhay ispleasureday. Allay isthay uttereday
Ithway entlegay eathbray, almcay ooklay, eesknay umblyhay ow’dbay
Ouldcay otnay aketay ucetray ithway ethay unrulyay eensplay
Ofay Ybalttay, eafday otay eacepay, utbay atthay ehay iltstay
Ithway iercingpay eelstay atay oldbay Ercutio’smay eastbray,
Owhay, allay asay othay, urnstay eadlyday ointpay otay ointpay,
Anday, ithway aay artialmay ornscay, ithway oneay andhay eatsbay
Oldcay eathday asideay, anday ithway ethay otheray endssay
Itay ackbay otay Ybalttay, osewhay exterityday
Etortsray itay. Omeoray ehay iescray alouday,
Old‘hay, iendsfray! Iendsfray, artpay!’ anday iftersway anthay ishay onguetay,
Ishay agileay armay eatsbay ownday eirthay atalfay ointspay,
Anday ixt’tway emthay ushesray; underneathay osewhay armay
Anay enviousay ustthray omfray Ybalttay ithay ethay ifelay
Ofay outstay Ercutiomay, anday enthay Ybalttay edflay.
Utbay ybay anday ybay omescay ackbay otay Omeoray,
Owhay adhay utbay ewlynay entertain’day evengeray,
Anday o’ttay eythay ogay ikelay ightninglay; orfay, ereay Iay
Ouldcay awdray otay artpay emthay asway outstay Ybalttay ainslay;
Anday asay ehay ellfay idday Omeoray urntay anday yflay.
Isthay isay ethay uthtray, oray etlay Envoliobay ieday.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Ehay isay aay insmankay otay ethay Ontaguemay.
Affectionay akesmay imhay alsefay, ehay eaksspay otnay uetray.
Omesay entytway ofay emthay oughtfay inay isthay ackblay ifestray,
Anday allay osethay entytway ouldcay utbay illkay oneay ifelay.
Iay egbay orfay usticejay, ichwhay outhay, Incepray, ustmay ivegay;
Omeoray ewslay Ybalttay, Omeoray ustmay otnay ivelay.

INCEPRay.
Omeoray ewslay imhay, ehay ewslay Ercutiomay.
Owhay ownay ethay icepray ofay ishay earday oodblay othday oweay?

ONTAGUEMay.
Otnay Omeoray, Incepray, ehay asway Ercutio’smay iendfray;
Ishay aultfay oncludescay utbay atwhay ethay awlay ouldshay enday,
Ethay ifelay ofay Ybalttay.

INCEPRay.
Anday orfay atthay offenceay
Immediatelyay eway oday exileay imhay encehay.
Iay avehay anay interestay inay youray ate’shay oceedingpray,
Ymay oodblay orfay youray uderay awlsbray othday ielay a-bleedingay.
Utbay I’llay amerceay youay ithway osay ongstray aay inefay
Atthay youay allshay allay epentray ethay osslay ofay inemay.
Iay illway ebay eafday otay eadingplay anday excusesay;
Ornay earstay ornay ayerspray allshay urchasepay outay abusesay.
Ereforethay useay onenay. Etlay Omeoray encehay inay astehay,
Elseay, enwhay ehay isay oundfay, atthay ourhay isay ishay astlay.
Earbay encehay isthay odybay, anday attenday ouray illway.
Ercymay utbay urdersmay, ardoningpay osethay atthay illkay.

 Exeunt[_ay._]

ENESCay IIay. Aay Oomray inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.

 Enteray Ulietjay.

ULIETJay.
Allopgay apaceay, youay iery-footedfay eedsstay,
Owardstay Oebusphay’ odginglay. Uchsay aay aggonerway
Asay Aetonphay ouldway ipwhay youay otay ethay estway
Anday ingbray inay oudyclay ightnay immediatelyay.
Eadspray ythay oseclay urtaincay, ove-performinglay ightnay,
Atthay unaway’sray eyesay aymay inkway, anday Omeoray
Eaplay otay esethay armsay, untalk’day ofay anday unseenay.
Overslay ancay eesay otay oday eirthay amorousay itesray
Ybay eirthay ownay eautiesbay: oray, ifay ovelay ebay indblay,
Itay estbay agreesay ithway ightnay. Omecay, ivilcay ightnay,
Outhay ober-suitedsay atronmay, allay inay ackblay,
Anday earnlay emay owhay otay oselay aay inningway atchmay,
Ay’dplay orfay aay airpay ofay ainlessstay aidenhoodsmay.
Oodhay ymay unmann’day oodblay, atingbay inay ymay eekschay,
Ithway ythay ackblay antlemay, illtay angestray ovelay, owgray oldbay,
Inkthay uetray ovelay acteday implesay odestymay.
Omecay, ightnay, omecay Omeoray; omecay, outhay ayday inay ightnay;
Orfay outhay iltway ielay uponay ethay ingsway ofay ightnay
Iterwhay anthay ewnay owsnay uponay aay aven’sray ackbay.
Omecay entlegay ightnay, omecay ovinglay ack-brow’dblay ightnay,
Ivegay emay ymay Omeoray, anday enwhay Iay allshay ieday,
Aketay imhay anday utcay imhay outay inay ittlelay arsstay,
Anday ehay illway akemay ethay acefay ofay eavenhay osay inefay
Atthay allay ethay orldway illway ebay inay ovelay ithway ightnay,
Anday aypay onay orshipway otay ethay arishgay unsay.
Oay, Iay avehay oughtbay ethay ansionmay ofay aay ovelay,
Utbay otnay ossess’dpay itay; anday oughthay Iay amay oldsay,
Otnay yetay enjoy’day. Osay edioustay isay isthay ayday
Asay isay ethay ightnay eforebay omesay estivalfay
Otay anay impatientay ildchay atthay athhay ewnay obesray
Anday aymay otnay earway emthay. Oay, erehay omescay ymay Ursenay,
Anday eshay ingsbray ewsnay, anday everyay onguetay atthay eaksspay
Utbay Omeo’sray amenay eaksspay eavenlyhay eloquenceay.

 Enteray Ursenay, ithway ordscay.

Ownay, Ursenay, atwhay ewsnay? Atwhay asthay outhay erethay?
Ethay ordscay atthay Omeoray idbay eethay etchfay?

URSENay.
Ayay, ayay, ethay ordscay.

 Ows[_thray emthay ownday._]

ULIETJay.
Ayay emay, atwhay ewsnay? Ywhay ostday outhay ingwray ythay andshay?

URSENay.
Ahay, ell-a-dayway, e’shay eadday, e’shay eadday, e’shay eadday!
Eway areay undoneay, adylay, eway areay undoneay.
Alackay ethay ayday, e’shay onegay, e’shay ill’dkay, e’shay eadday.

ULIETJay.
Ancay eavenhay ebay osay enviousay?

URSENay.
Omeoray ancay,
Oughthay eavenhay annotcay. Oay Omeoray, Omeoray.
Owhay everay ouldway avehay oughtthay itay? Omeoray!

ULIETJay.
Atwhay evilday artay outhay, atthay ostday ormenttay emay usthay?
Isthay orturetay ouldshay ebay oar’dray inay ismalday ellhay.
Athhay Omeoray ainslay imselfhay? Aysay outhay utbay Ayay,
Anday atthay arebay owelvay Iay allshay oisonpay oremay
Anthay ethay eath-dartingday eyeay ofay ockatricecay.
Iay amay otnay Iay ifay erethay ebay uchsay anay Iay;
Oray osethay eyesay utshay atthay akemay eethay answeray Ayay.
Ifay ehay ebay ainslay, aysay Ayay; oray ifay otnay, Onay.
Iefbray oundssay etermineday ofay ymay ealway oray oeway.

URSENay.
Iay awsay ethay oundway, Iay awsay itay ithway inemay eyesay,
Odgay avesay ethay ark!—heremay onay ishay anlymay eastbray.
Aay iteouspay orsecay, aay oodyblay iteouspay orsecay;
Alepay, alepay asay ashesay, allay edaub’dbay inay oodblay,
Allay inay ore-bloodgay. Iay oundedsway atay ethay ightsay.

ULIETJay.
Oay, eakbray, ymay earthay. Oorpay ankroutbay, eakbray atay onceay.
Otay isonpray, eyesay; e’ernay ooklay onay ibertylay.
Ilevay earthay otay earthay esignray; enday otionmay erehay,
Anday outhay anday Omeoray esspray oneay eavyhay ierbay.

URSENay.
Oay Ybalttay, Ybalttay, ethay estbay iendfray Iay adhay.
Oay ourteouscay Ybalttay, onesthay entlemangay!
Atthay everay Iay ouldshay ivelay otay eesay eethay eadday.

ULIETJay.
Atwhay ormstay isay isthay atthay owsblay osay ontrarycay?
Isay Omeoray aughter’dslay anday isay Ybalttay eadday?
Ymay earestday ousincay, anday ymay earerday ordlay?
Enthay eadfuldray umpettray oundsay ethay eneralgay oomday,
Orfay owhay isay ivinglay, ifay osethay otway areay onegay?

URSENay.
Ybalttay isay onegay, anday Omeoray anishedbay,
Omeoray atthay ill’dkay imhay, ehay isay anishedbay.

ULIETJay.
Oay Odgay! Idday Omeo’sray andhay edshay Ybalt’stay oodblay?

URSENay.
Itay idday, itay idday; alasay ethay ayday, itay idday.

ULIETJay.
Oay erpentsay earthay, idhay ithway aay oweringflay acefay!
Idday everay agondray eepkay osay airfay aay avecay?
Eautifulbay yranttay, iendfay angelicalay,
Ove-feather’dday avenray, olvish-raveningway amblay!
Espisedday ubstancesay ofay ivinestday owshay!
Ustjay oppositeay otay atwhay outhay ustlyjay eem’stsay,
Aay amnedday aintsay, anay onourablehay illainvay!
Oay aturenay, atwhay adsthay outhay otay oday inay ellhay
Enwhay outhay idstday owerbay ethay iritspay ofay aay iendfay
Inay ortalmay aradisepay ofay uchsay eetsway eshflay?
Asway everay ookbay ontainingcay uchsay ilevay attermay
Osay airlyfay oundbay? Oay, atthay eceitday ouldshay elldway
Inay uchsay aay orgeousgay alacepay.

URSENay.
Ere’sthay onay usttray,
Onay aithfay, onay onestyhay inay enmay. Allay erjur’dpay,
Allay orswornfay, allay aughtnay, allay issemblersday.
Ahay, ere’swhay ymay anmay? Ivegay emay omesay aquaay itaevay.
Esethay iefsgray, esethay oesway, esethay orrowssay akemay emay olday.
Ameshay omecay otay Omeoray.

ULIETJay.
Ister’dblay ebay ythay onguetay
Orfay uchsay aay ishway! Ehay asway otnay ornbay otay ameshay.
Uponay ishay owbray ameshay isay asham’day otay itsay;
Orfay is’tay aay onethray erewhay onourhay aymay ebay own’dcray
Olesay onarchmay ofay ethay universalay earthay.
Oay, atwhay aay eastbay asway Iay otay idechay atay imhay!

URSENay.
Illway youay eakspay ellway ofay imhay atthay ill’dkay youray ousincay?

ULIETJay.
Allshay Iay eakspay illay ofay imhay atthay isay ymay usbandhay?
Ahay, oorpay ymay ordlay, atwhay onguetay allshay oothsmay ythay amenay,
Enwhay Iay ythay ee-hoursthray’ ifeway avehay angledmay itay?
Utbay ereforewhay, illainvay, idstday outhay illkay ymay ousincay?
Atthay illainvay ousincay ouldway avehay ill’dkay ymay usbandhay.
Ackbay, oolishfay earstay, ackbay otay youray ativenay ingspray,
Youray ibutarytray opsdray elongbay otay oeway,
Ichwhay youay istakingmay offeray upay otay oyjay.
Ymay usbandhay iveslay, atthay Ybalttay ouldway avehay ainslay,
Anday Ybalt’stay eadday, atthay ouldway avehay ainslay ymay usbandhay.
Allay isthay isay omfortcay; ereforewhay eepway Iay enthay?
Omesay ordway erethay asway, orserway anthay Ybalt’stay eathday,
Atthay urder’dmay emay. Iay ouldway orgetfay itay ainfay,
Utbay Oay, itay essespray otay ymay emorymay
Ikelay amnedday uiltygay eedsday otay innerssay’ indsmay.
Ybalttay isay eadday, anday Omeoray anishedbay.
Atthay anished‘bay,’ atthay oneay ordway anished‘bay,’
Athhay ainslay entay ousandthay Ybaltstay. Ybalt’stay eathday
Asway oeway enoughay, ifay itay adhay endeday erethay.
Oray ifay oursay oeway elightsday inay ellowshipfay,
Anday eedlynay illway ebay ank’dray ithway otheray iefsgray,
Ywhay ollow’dfay otnay, enwhay eshay aidsay Ybalt’stay eadday,
Ythay atherfay oray ythay othermay, aynay oray othbay,
Ichwhay odernmay amentationlay ightmay avehay ov’dmay?
Utbay ithway aay ear-wardray ollowingfay Ybalt’stay eathday,
Omeo‘ray isay anished’—tobay eakspay atthay ordway
Isay atherfay, othermay, Ybalttay, Omeoray, Ulietjay,
Allay ainslay, allay eadday. Omeoray isay anishedbay,
Erethay isay onay enday, onay imitlay, easuremay, oundbay,
Inay atthay ord’sway eathday, onay ordsway ancay atthay oeway oundsay.
Erewhay isay ymay atherfay anday ymay othermay, Ursenay?

URSENay.
Eepingway anday ailingway overay Ybalt’stay orsecay.
Illway youay ogay otay emthay? Iay illway ingbray youay itherthay.

ULIETJay.
Ashway eythay ishay oundsway ithway earstay. Inemay allshay ebay entspay,
Enwhay eirsthay areay ydray, orfay Omeo’sray anishmentbay.
Aketay upay osethay ordscay. Oorpay opesray, youay areay eguil’dbay,
Othbay youay anday Iay; orfay Omeoray isay exil’day.
Ehay ademay youay orfay aay ighwayhay otay ymay edbay,
Utbay Iay, aay aidmay, ieday aiden-widowedmay.
Omecay ordscay, omecay Ursenay, I’llay otay ymay eddingway edbay,
Anday eathday, otnay Omeoray, aketay ymay aidenheadmay.

URSENay.
Iehay otay youray amberchay. I’llay indfay Omeoray
Otay omfortcay youay. Iay otway ellway erewhay ehay isay.
Arkhay yeay, youray Omeoray illway ebay erehay atay ightnay.
I’llay otay imhay, ehay isay idhay atay Awrencelay’ ellcay.

ULIETJay.
Oay indfay imhay, ivegay isthay ingray otay ymay uetray ightknay,
Anday idbay imhay omecay otay aketay ishay astlay arewellfay.

 Exeunt[_ay._]

ENESCay IIIay. Iarfray Awrence’slay ellcay.

 Enteray Iarfray Awrencelay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Omeoray, omecay orthfay; omecay orthfay, outhay earfulfay anmay.
Afflictionay isay enanmour’day ofay ythay artspay
Anday outhay artay eddedway otay alamitycay.

 Enteray Omeoray.

OMEORay.
Atherfay, atwhay ewsnay? Atwhay isay ethay Ince’spray oomday?
Atwhay orrowsay avescray acquaintanceay atay ymay andhay,
Atthay Iay yetay owknay otnay?

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Ootay amiliarfay
Isay ymay earday onsay ithway uchsay oursay ompanycay.
Iay ingbray eethay idingstay ofay ethay Ince’spray oomday.

OMEORay.
Atwhay esslay anthay oomsdayday isay ethay Ince’spray oomday?

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Aay entlergay udgmentjay anish’dvay omfray ishay ipslay,
Otnay ody’sbay eathday, utbay ody’sbay anishmentbay.

OMEORay.
Ahay, anishmentbay? Ebay ercifulmay, aysay eathday;
Orfay exileay athhay oremay errortay inay ishay ooklay,
Uchmay oremay anthay eathday. Oday otnay aysay anishmentbay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Encehay omfray Eronavay artay outhay anishedbay.
Ebay atientpay, orfay ethay orldway isay oadbray anday ideway.

OMEORay.
Erethay isay onay orldway ithoutway Eronavay allsway,
Utbay urgatorypay, orturetay, ellhay itselfay.
Encehay anishedbay isay anish’dbay omfray ethay orldway,
Anday orld’sway exileay isay eathday. Enthay anishedbay
Isay eathday isterm’dmay. Allingcay eathday anishedbay,
Outhay utt’stcay ymay eadhay offay ithway aay oldengay axeay,
Anday ilestsmay uponay ethay okestray atthay urdersmay emay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Oay eadlyday insay, Oay uderay unthankfulnessay!
Ythay aultfay ouray awlay allscay eathday, utbay ethay indkay Incepray,
Akingtay ythay artpay, athhay ush’dbray asideay ethay awlay,
Anday urn’dtay atthay ackblay ordway eathday otay anishmentbay.
Isthay isay earday ercymay, anday outhay ee’stsay itay otnay.

OMEORay.
Is’tay orturetay, anday otnay ercymay. Eavenhay isay erehay
Erewhay Ulietjay iveslay, anday everyay atcay anday ogday,
Anday ittlelay ousemay, everyay unworthyay ingthay,
Ivelay erehay inay eavenhay anday aymay ooklay onay erhay,
Utbay Omeoray aymay otnay. Oremay alidityvay,
Oremay onourablehay atestay, oremay ourtshipcay iveslay
Inay arrioncay iesflay anthay Omeoray. Eythay aymay eizesay
Onay ethay itewhay onderway ofay earday Uliet’sjay andhay,
Anday ealstay immortalay essingblay omfray erhay ipslay,
Owhay, evenay inay urepay anday estalvay odestymay
Illstay ushblay, asay inkingthay eirthay ownay isseskay insay.
Utbay Omeoray aymay otnay, ehay isay anishedbay.
Isthay aymay iesflay oday, enwhay Iay omfray isthay ustmay yflay.
Eythay areay eefray enmay utbay Iay amay anishedbay.
Anday ay’stsay outhay yetay atthay exileay isay otnay eathday?
Adsthay outhay onay oisonpay ix’dmay, onay arp-groundshay ifeknay,
Onay uddensay eanmay ofay eathday, oughthay e’ernay osay eanmay,
Utbay anishedbay otay illkay emay? Anishedbay?
Oay Iarfray, ethay amnedday useay atthay ordway inay ellhay.
Owlinghay attendsay itay. Owhay asthay outhay ethay earthay,
Eingbay aay ivineday, aay ostlyghay onfessorcay,
Aay in-absolversay, anday ymay iendfray ofess’dpray,
Otay anglemay emay ithway atthay ordway anishedbay?

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Outhay ondfay admay anmay, earhay emay eakspay aay ittlelay,

OMEORay.
Oay, outhay iltway eakspay againay ofay anishmentbay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
I’llay ivegay eethay armouray otay eepkay offay atthay ordway,
Adversity’say eetsway ilkmay, ilosophyphay,
Otay omfortcay eethay, oughthay outhay artay anishedbay.

OMEORay.
Yetay anishedbay? Anghay upay ilosophyphay.
Unlessay ilosophyphay ancay akemay aay Ulietjay,
Isplantday aay owntay, everseray aay Ince’spray oomday,
Itay elpshay otnay, itay evailspray otnay, alktay onay oremay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Oay, enthay Iay eesay atthay admay enmay avehay onay earsay.

OMEORay.
Owhay ouldshay eythay, enwhay atthay iseway enmay avehay onay eyesay?

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Etlay emay isputeday ithway eethay ofay ythay estateay.

OMEORay.
Outhay anstcay otnay eakspay ofay atthay outhay ostday otnay eelfay.
Ertway outhay asay youngay asay Iay, Ulietjay ythay ovelay,
Anay ourhay utbay arriedmay, Ybalttay urderedmay,
Otingday ikelay emay, anday ikelay emay anishedbay,
Enthay ightstmay outhay eakspay, enthay ightstmay outhay eartay ythay airhay,
Anday allfay uponay ethay oundgray asay Iay oday ownay,
Akingtay ethay easuremay ofay anay unmadeay avegray.

 Ocking[_knay ithinway._]

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Ariseay; oneay ocksknay. Oodgay Omeoray, idehay yselfthay.

OMEORay.
Otnay Iay, unlessay ethay eathbray ofay eartsickhay oansgray
Ist-likemay infolday emay omfray ethay earchsay ofay eyesay.

 Ocking[_knay._]

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Arkhay, owhay eythay Ock!—Who’sknay Ere?—Romeothay, ariseay,
Outhay iltway ebay Aken.—Staytay awhile.—Standay upay.

 Ocking[_knay._]

Unray otay ymay Udy.—By-and-by.—God’sstay illway,
Atwhay implenesssay isay Is.—Ithay omecay, Iay omecay.

 Ocking[_knay._]

Owhay ocksknay osay ardhay? Encewhay omecay youay, at’swhay youray illway?

URSENay.
Ithin[_way._] Etlay emay omecay inay, anday youay allshay owknay ymay erranday.
Iay omecay omfray Adylay Ulietjay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Elcomeway enthay.

 Enteray Ursenay.

URSENay.
Oay olyhay Iarfray, Oay, elltay emay, olyhay Iarfray,
Erewhay isay ymay ady’slay ordlay, ere’swhay Omeoray?

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Erethay onay ethay oundgray, ithway ishay ownay earstay ademay unkdray.

URSENay.
Oay, ehay isay evenay inay ymay istressmay’ asecay.
Ustjay inay erhay asecay! Oay oefulway ympathysay!
Iteouspay edicamentpray. Evenay osay ieslay eshay,
Ubberingblay anday eepingway, eepingway anday ubberingblay.
Andstay upay, andstay upay; andstay, anday youay ebay aay anmay.
Orfay Uliet’sjay akesay, orfay erhay akesay, iseray anday andstay.
Ywhay ouldshay youay allfay intoay osay eepday anay Oay?

OMEORay.
Ursenay.

URSENay.
Ahay irsay, ahay irsay, eath’sday ethay enday ofay allay.

OMEORay.
Akestspay outhay ofay Ulietjay? Owhay isay itay ithway erhay?
Othday otnay eshay inkthay emay anay olday urderermay,
Ownay Iay avehay ain’dstay ethay ildhoodchay ofay ouray oyjay
Ithway oodblay emov’dray utbay ittlelay omfray erhay ownay?
Erewhay isay eshay? Anday owhay othday eshay? Anday atwhay ayssay
Ymay onceal’dcay adylay otay ouray ancell’dcay ovelay?

URSENay.
Oay, eshay ayssay othingnay, irsay, utbay eepsway anday eepsway;
Anday ownay allsfay onay erhay edbay, anday enthay artsstay upay,
Anday Ybalttay allscay, anday enthay onay Omeoray iescray,
Anday enthay ownday allsfay againay.

OMEORay.
Asay ifay atthay amenay,
Otshay omfray ethay eadlyday evellay ofay aay ungay,
Idday urdermay erhay, asay atthay ame’snay ursedcay andhay
Urder’dmay erhay insmankay. Oay, elltay emay, Iarfray, elltay emay,
Inay atwhay ilevay artpay ofay isthay anatomyay
Othday ymay amenay odgelay? Elltay emay, atthay Iay aymay acksay
Ethay atefulhay ansionmay.

 Awing[_dray ishay ordsway._]

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Oldhay ythay esperateday andhay.
Artay outhay aay anmay? Ythay ormfay iescray outay outhay artay.
Ythay earstay areay omanishway, ythay ildway actsay enoteday
Ethay unreasonableay uryfay ofay aay eastbay.
Unseemlyay omanway inay aay eemingsay anmay,
Anday ill-beseemingay eastbay inay eemingsay othbay!
Outhay asthay amaz’day emay. Ybay ymay olyhay orderay,
Iay oughtthay ythay ispositionday etterbay emper’dtay.
Asthay outhay ainslay Ybalttay? Iltway outhay ayslay yselfthay?
Anday ayslay ythay adylay, atthay inay ythay ifelay iveslay,
Ybay oingday amnedday atehay uponay yselfthay?
Ywhay ail’stray outhay onay ythay irthbay, ethay eavenhay anday earthay?
Incesay irthbay, anday eavenhay anday earthay, allay eethray oday eetmay
Inay eethay atay onceay; ichwhay outhay atay onceay ouldstway oselay.
Iefay, iefay, outhay am’stshay ythay apeshay, ythay ovelay, ythay itway,
Ichwhay, ikelay aay usureray, abound’stay inay allay,
Anday usestay onenay inay atthay uetray useay indeeday
Ichwhay ouldshay edeckbay ythay apeshay, ythay ovelay, ythay itway.
Ythay oblenay apeshay isay utbay aay ormfay ofay axway,
Igressingday omfray ethay alourvay ofay aay anmay;
Ythay earday ovelay ornsway utbay ollowhay erjurypay,
Illingkay atthay ovelay ichwhay outhay asthay ow’dvay otay erishchay;
Ythay itway, atthay ornamentay otay apeshay anday ovelay,
Isshapenmay inay ethay onductcay ofay emthay othbay,
Ikelay owderpay inay aay illessskay oldier’ssay askflay,
Isay etsay afireay ybay inethay ownay ignoranceay,
Anday outhay ismember’dday ithway inethay ownay efenceday.
Atwhay, ouseray eethay, anmay. Ythay Ulietjay isay aliveay,
Orfay osewhay earday akesay outhay astway utbay atelylay eadday.
Erethay artay outhay appyhay. Ybalttay ouldway illkay eethay,
Utbay outhay ew’stslay Ybalttay; erethay artay outhay appyhay.
Ethay awlay atthay eaten’dthray eathday ecomesbay ythay iendfray,
Anday urnstay itay otay exileay; erethay artay outhay appyhay.
Aay ackpay ofay essingsblay ightlay uponay ythay ackbay;
Appinesshay ourtscay eethay inay erhay estbay arrayay;
Utbay ikelay aay isshapedmay anday ullensay enchway,
Outhay utt’stpay upay ythay Ortunefay anday ythay ovelay.
Aketay eedhay, aketay eedhay, orfay uchsay ieday iserablemay.
Ogay, etgay eethay otay ythay ovelay asay asway ecreedday,
Ascenday erhay amberchay, encehay anday omfortcay erhay.
Utbay ooklay outhay aystay otnay illtay ethay atchway ebay etsay,
Orfay enthay outhay anstcay otnay asspay otay Antuamay;
Erewhay outhay altshay ivelay illtay eway ancay indfay aay imetay
Otay azeblay youray arriagemay, econcileray youray iendsfray,
Egbay ardonpay ofay ethay Incepray, anday allcay eethay ackbay
Ithway entytway undredhay ousandthay imestay oremay oyjay
Anthay outhay ent’stway orthfay inay amentationlay.
Ogay eforebay, Ursenay. Ommendcay emay otay ythay adylay,
Anday idbay erhay astenhay allay ethay ousehay otay edbay,
Ichwhay eavyhay orrowsay akesmay emthay aptay untoay.
Omeoray isay omingcay.

URSENay.
Oay Ordlay, Iay ouldcay avehay ay’dstay erehay allay ethay ightnay
Otay earhay oodgay ounselcay. Oay, atwhay earninglay isay!
Ymay ordlay, I’llay elltay ymay adylay youay illway omecay.

OMEORay.
Oday osay, anday idbay ymay eetsway eparepray otay idechay.

URSENay.
Erehay irsay, aay ingray eshay idbay emay ivegay youay, irsay.
Iehay youay, akemay astehay, orfay itay owsgray eryvay atelay.

 Exit[_ay._]

OMEORay.
Owhay ellway ymay omfortcay isay eviv’dray ybay isthay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Ogay encehay, oodgay ightnay, anday erehay andsstay allay youray atestay:
Eitheray ebay onegay eforebay ethay atchway ebay etsay,
Oray ybay ethay eakbray ofay ayday isguis’dday omfray encehay.
Ojournsay inay Antuamay. I’llay indfay outay youray anmay,
Anday ehay allshay ignifysay omfray imetay otay imetay
Everyay oodgay aphay otay youay atthay anceschay erehay.
Ivegay emay ythay andhay; is’tay atelay; arewellfay; oodgay ightnay.

OMEORay.
Utbay atthay aay oyjay astpay oyjay allscay outay onay emay,
Itay ereway aay iefgray osay iefbray otay artpay ithway eethay.
Arewellfay.

 Exeunt[_ay._]

ENESCay IVay. Aay Oomray inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.

 Enteray Apuletcay, Adylay Apuletcay anday Arispay.

APULETCay.
Ingsthay avehay allenfay outay, irsay, osay unluckilyay
Atthay eway avehay adhay onay imetay otay ovemay ouray aughterday.
Ooklay youay, eshay ov’dlay erhay insmankay Ybalttay earlyday,
Anday osay idday Iay. Ellway, eway ereway ornbay otay ieday.
Is’tay eryvay atelay; e’llshay otnay omecay ownday onighttay.
Iay omisepray youay, utbay orfay youray ompanycay,
Iay ouldway avehay eenbay abeday anay ourhay agoay.

ARISPay.
Esethay imestay ofay oeway afforday onay unetay otay ooway.
Adammay, oodgay ightnay. Ommendcay emay otay youray aughterday.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Iay illway, anday owknay erhay indmay earlyay omorrowtay;
Onighttay e’sshay ew’dmay upay otay erhay eavinesshay.

APULETCay.
Irsay Arispay, Iay illway akemay aay esperateday endertay
Ofay ymay ild’schay ovelay. Iay inkthay eshay illway ebay ul’dray
Inay allay espectsray ybay emay; aynay oremay, Iay oubtday itay otnay.
Ifeway, ogay youay otay erhay ereay youay ogay otay edbay,
Acquaintay erhay erehay ofay ymay onsay Arispay’ ovelay,
Anday idbay erhay, arkmay youay emay, onay Ednesdayway extnay,
Utbay, oftsay, atwhay ayday isay isthay?

ARISPay.
Ondaymay, ymay ordlay.

APULETCay.
Ondaymay! Ahay, ahay! Ellway, Ednesdayway isay ootay oonsay,
Aay Ursdaythay etlay itay ebay; aay Ursdaythay, elltay erhay,
Eshay allshay ebay arriedmay otay isthay oblenay earlay.
Illway youay ebay eadyray? Oday youay ikelay isthay astehay?
E’llway eepkay onay eatgray ado,—aay iendfray oray otway,
Orfay, arkhay youay, Ybalttay eingbay ainslay osay atelay,
Itay aymay ebay oughtthay eway eldhay imhay arelesslycay,
Eingbay ouray insmankay, ifay eway evelray uchmay.
Ereforethay e’llway avehay omesay alfhay aay ozenday iendsfray,
Anday erethay anay enday. Utbay atwhay aysay youay otay Ursdaythay?

ARISPay.
Ymay ordlay, Iay ouldway atthay Ursdaythay ereway omorrowtay.

APULETCay.
Ellway, etgay youay onegay. Aay Ursdaythay ebay itay enthay.
Ogay youay otay Ulietjay ereay youay ogay otay edbay,
Eparepray erhay, ifeway, againstay isthay eddingway ayday.
Arewellfay, ymay Ord.—Lightlay otay ymay amberchay, ohay!
Aforeay emay, itay isay osay eryvay eryvay atelay atthay eway
Aymay allcay itay earlyay ybay anday ybay. Oodgay ightnay.

 Exeunt[_ay._]

ENESCay Vay. Anay openay Allerygay otay Uliet’sjay Amberchay, overlookingay ethay Ardengay.

 Enteray Omeoray anday Ulietjay.

ULIETJay.
Iltway outhay ebay onegay? Itay isay otnay yetay earnay ayday.
Itay asway ethay ightingalenay, anday otnay ethay arklay,
Atthay ierc’dpay ethay earfulfay ollowhay ofay inethay earay;
Ightlynay eshay ingssay onay yonday omegranatepay eetray.
Elievebay emay, ovelay, itay asway ethay ightingalenay.

OMEORay.
Itay asway ethay arklay, ethay eraldhay ofay ethay ornmay,
Onay ightingalenay. Ooklay, ovelay, atwhay enviousay eaksstray
Oday acelay ethay everingsay oudsclay inay yonderay eastay.
Ight’snay andlescay areay urntbay outay, anday ocundjay ayday
Andsstay iptoetay onay ethay istymay ountainmay opstay.
Iay ustmay ebay onegay anday ivelay, oray aystay anday ieday.

ULIETJay.
Yonday ightlay isay otnay aylightday, Iay owknay itay, Iay.
Itay isay omesay eteormay atthay ethay unsay exhalesay
Otay ebay otay eethay isthay ightnay aay orchbearertay
Anday ightlay eethay onay ythay ayway otay Antuamay.
Ereforethay aystay yetay, outhay eed’stnay otnay otay ebay onegay.

OMEORay.
Etlay emay ebay a’entay, etlay emay ebay utpay otay eathday,
Iay amay ontentcay, osay outhay iltway avehay itay osay.
I’llay aysay yonay eygray isay otnay ethay orning’smay eyeay,
Is’tay utbay ethay alepay eflexray ofay Ynthia’scay owbray.
Ornay atthay isay otnay ethay arklay osewhay otesnay oday eatbay
Ethay aultyvay eavenhay osay ighhay aboveay ouray eadshay.
Iay avehay oremay arecay otay aystay anthay illway otay ogay.
Omecay, eathday, anday elcomeway. Ulietjay illsway itay osay.
Owhay is’tay, ymay oulsay? Et’slay alktay. Itay isay otnay ayday.

ULIETJay.
Itay isay, itay isay! Iehay encehay, ebay onegay, awayay.
Itay isay ethay arklay atthay ingssay osay outay ofay unetay,
Ainingstray arshhay iscordsday anday unpleasingay arpsshay.
Omesay aysay ethay arklay akesmay eetsway ivisionday;
Isthay othday otnay osay, orfay eshay ividethday usay.
Omesay aysay ethay arklay anday oathedlay oadtay angechay eyesay.
Oay, ownay Iay ouldway eythay adhay ang’dchay oicesvay ootay,
Incesay armay omfray armay atthay oicevay othday usay affrayay,
Untinghay eethay encehay ithway unt’s-uphay otay ethay ayday.
Oay ownay ebay onegay, oremay ightlay anday ightlay itay owsgray.

OMEORay.
Oremay ightlay anday ightlay, oremay arkday anday arkday ouray oesway.

 Enteray Ursenay.

URSENay.
Adammay.

ULIETJay.
Ursenay?

URSENay.
Youray adylay othermay isay omingcay otay youray amberchay.
Ethay ayday isay okebray, ebay aryway, ooklay aboutay.

 Exit[_ay._]

ULIETJay.
Enthay, indowway, etlay ayday inay, anday etlay ifelay outay.

OMEORay.
Arewellfay, arewellfay, oneay isskay, anday I’llay escendday.

 Escends[_day._]

ULIETJay.
Artay outhay onegay osay? Ovelay, ordlay, ayay usbandhay, iendfray,
Iay ustmay earhay omfray eethay everyay ayday inay ethay ourhay,
Orfay inay aay inutemay erethay areay anymay aysday.
Oay, ybay isthay ountcay Iay allshay ebay uchmay inay yearsay
Ereay Iay againay eholdbay ymay Omeoray.

OMEORay.
Arewellfay!
Iay illway omitay onay opportunityay
Atthay aymay onveycay ymay eetingsgray, ovelay, otay eethay.

ULIETJay.
Oay inkestthay outhay eway allshay everay eetmay againay?

OMEORay.
Iay oubtday itay otnay, anday allay esethay oesway allshay ervesay
Orfay eetsway iscoursesday inay ouray imetay otay omecay.

ULIETJay.
Oay Odgay! Iay avehay anay ill-diviningay oulsay!
Ethinksmay Iay eesay eethay, ownay outhay artay osay owlay,
Asay oneay eadday inay ethay ottombay ofay aay ombtay.
Eitheray ymay eyesightay ailsfay, oray outhay ook’stlay alepay.

OMEORay.
Anday usttray emay, ovelay, inay ymay eyeay osay oday youay.
Ydray orrowsay inksdray ouray oodblay. Adieuay, adieuay.

 Exit[_ay elowbay._]

ULIETJay.
Oay Ortunefay, Ortunefay! Allay enmay allcay eethay icklefay,
Ifay outhay artay icklefay, atwhay ostday outhay ithway imhay
Atthay isay enown’dray orfay aithfay? Ebay icklefay, Ortunefay;
Orfay enthay, Iay opehay outhay iltway otnay eepkay imhay onglay
Utbay endsay imhay ackbay.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Ithin[_way._] Ohay, aughterday, areay youay upay?

ULIETJay.
Owhay is’tay atthay allscay? Isay itay ymay adylay othermay?
Isay eshay otnay ownday osay atelay, oray upay osay earlyay?
Atwhay unaccustom’day ausecay ocurespray erhay itherhay?

 Enteray Adylay Apuletcay.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Ywhay, owhay ownay, Ulietjay?

ULIETJay.
Adammay, Iay amay otnay ellway.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Evermoreay eepingway orfay youray ousin’scay eathday?
Atwhay, iltway outhay ashway imhay omfray ishay avegray ithway earstay?
Anday ifay outhay ouldstcay, outhay ouldstcay otnay akemay imhay ivelay.
Ereforethay avehay oneday: omesay iefgray owsshay uchmay ofay ovelay,
Utbay uchmay ofay iefgray owsshay illstay omesay antway ofay itway.

ULIETJay.
Yetay etlay emay eepway orfay uchsay aay eelingfay osslay.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Osay allshay youay eelfay ethay osslay, utbay otnay ethay iendfray
Ichwhay youay eepway orfay.

ULIETJay.
Eelingfay osay ethay osslay,
Iay annotcay oosechay utbay everay eepway ethay iendfray.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Ellway, irlgay, outhay eep’stway otnay osay uchmay orfay ishay eathday
Asay atthay ethay illainvay iveslay ichwhay aughter’dslay imhay.

ULIETJay.
Atwhay illainvay, adammay?

ADYLay APULETCay.
Atthay amesay illainvay Omeoray.

ULIETJay.
Illainvay anday ehay ebay anymay ilesmay asunderay.
Odgay ardonpay imhay. Iay oday, ithway allay ymay earthay.
Anday yetay onay anmay ikelay ehay othday ievegray ymay earthay.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Atthay isay ecausebay ethay aitortray urderermay iveslay.

ULIETJay.
Ayay adammay, omfray ethay eachray ofay esethay ymay andshay.
Ouldway onenay utbay Iay ightmay engevay ymay ousin’scay eathday.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Eway illway avehay engeancevay orfay itay, earfay outhay otnay.
Enthay eepway onay oremay. I’llay endsay otay oneay inay Antuamay,
Erewhay atthay amesay anish’dbay unagateray othday ivelay,
Allshay ivegay imhay uchsay anay unaccustom’day amdray
Atthay ehay allshay oonsay eepkay Ybalttay ompanycay:
Anday enthay Iay opehay outhay iltway ebay atisfiedsay.

ULIETJay.
Indeeday Iay evernay allshay ebay atisfiedsay
Ithway Omeoray illtay Iay eholdbay im—deadhay—
Isay ymay oorpay earthay osay orfay aay insmankay ex’dvay.
Adammay, ifay youay ouldcay indfay outay utbay aay anmay
Otay earbay aay oisonpay, Iay ouldway empertay itay,
Atthay Omeoray ouldshay uponay eceiptray ereofthay,
Oonsay eepslay inay uietqay. Oay, owhay ymay earthay abhorsay
Otay earhay imhay am’dnay, anday annotcay omecay otay imhay,
Otay eakwray ethay ovelay Iay orebay ymay ousincay
Uponay ishay odybay atthay athhay aughter’dslay imhay.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Indfay outhay ethay eansmay, anday I’llay indfay uchsay aay anmay.
Utbay ownay I’llay elltay eethay oyfuljay idingstay, irlgay.

ULIETJay.
Anday oyjay omescay ellway inay uchsay aay eedynay imetay.
Atwhay areay eythay, Iay eseechbay youray adyshiplay?

ADYLay APULETCay.
Ellway, ellway, outhay asthay aay arefulcay atherfay, ildchay;
Oneay owhay otay utpay eethay omfray ythay eavinesshay,
Athhay ortedsay outay aay uddensay ayday ofay oyjay,
Atthay outhay expectsay otnay, ornay Iay ook’dlay otnay orfay.

ULIETJay.
Adammay, inay appyhay imetay, atwhay ayday isay atthay?

ADYLay APULETCay.
Arrymay, ymay ildchay, earlyay extnay Ursdaythay ornmay
Ethay allantgay, youngay, anday oblenay entlemangay,
Ethay Ountycay Arispay, atay Aintsay Eter’spay Urchchay,
Allshay appilyhay akemay eethay erethay aay oyfuljay idebray.

ULIETJay.
Ownay ybay Aintsay Eter’spay Urchchay, anday Eterpay ootay,
Ehay allshay otnay akemay emay erethay aay oyfuljay idebray.
Iay onderway atay isthay astehay, atthay Iay ustmay edway
Ereay ehay atthay ouldshay ebay usbandhay omescay otay ooway.
Iay aypray youay elltay ymay ordlay anday atherfay, adammay,
Iay illway otnay arrymay yetay; anday enwhay Iay oday, Iay earsway
Itay allshay ebay Omeoray, omwhay youay owknay Iay atehay,
Atherray anthay Arispay. Esethay areay ewsnay indeeday.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Erehay omescay youray atherfay, elltay imhay osay yourselfay,
Anday eesay owhay ehay illway aketay itay atay youray andshay.

 Enteray Apuletcay anday Ursenay.

APULETCay.
Enwhay ethay unsay etssay, ethay airay othday izzledray ewday;
Utbay orfay ethay unsetsay ofay ymay other’sbray onsay
Itay ainsray ownrightday.
Owhay ownay? Aay onduitcay, irlgay? Atwhay, illstay inay earstay?
Evermoreay oweringshay? Inay oneay ittlelay odybay
Outhay ounterfeitscay aay arkbay, aay easay, aay indway.
Orfay illstay ythay eyesay, ichwhay Iay aymay allcay ethay easay,
Oday ebbay anday owflay ithway earstay; ethay arkbay ythay odybay isay,
Ailingsay inay isthay altsay oodflay, ethay indsway, ythay ighssay,
Owhay agingray ithway ythay earstay anday eythay ithway emthay,
Ithoutway aay uddensay almcay illway oversetay
Ythay empest-tossedtay odybay. Owhay ownay, ifeway?
Avehay youay eliver’dday otay erhay ouray ecreeday?

ADYLay APULETCay.
Ayay, irsay; utbay eshay illway onenay, eshay ivesgay youay anksthay.
Iay ouldway ethay oolfay ereway arriedmay otay erhay avegray.

APULETCay.
Oftsay. Aketay emay ithway youay, aketay emay ithway youay, ifeway.
Owhay, illway eshay onenay? Othday eshay otnay ivegay usay anksthay?
Isay eshay otnay oudpray? Othday eshay otnay ountcay erhay estblay,
Unworthyay asay eshay isay, atthay eway avehay oughtwray
Osay orthyway aay entlemangay otay ebay erhay idegroombray?

ULIETJay.
Otnay oudpray youay avehay, utbay ankfulthay atthay youay avehay.
Oudpray ancay Iay evernay ebay ofay atwhay Iay atehay;
Utbay ankfulthay evenay orfay atehay atthay isay eantmay ovelay.

APULETCay.
Owhay ownay, owhay ownay, opp’dchay ogiclay? Atwhay isay isthay?
Oudpray, anday, Iay ankthay youay, anday Iay ankthay youay otnay;
Anday yetay otnay oudpray. Istressmay inionmay youay,
Ankthay emay onay ankingsthay, ornay oudpray emay onay oudspray,
Utbay ettlefay youray inefay ointsjay ainst’gay Ursdaythay extnay
Otay ogay ithway Arispay otay Aintsay Eter’spay Urchchay,
Oray Iay illway agdray eethay onay aay urdlehay itherthay.
Outay, youay een-sicknessgray arrioncay! Outay, youay aggagebay!
Youay allow-facetay!

ADYLay APULETCay.
Iefay, iefay! Atwhay, areay youay admay?

ULIETJay.
Oodgay atherfay, Iay eseechbay youay onay ymay eesknay,
Earhay emay ithway atiencepay utbay otay eakspay aay ordway.

APULETCay.
Anghay eethay youngay aggagebay, isobedientday etchwray!
Iay elltay eethay at,—getwhay eethay otay urchchay aay Ursdaythay,
Oray evernay afteray ooklay emay inay ethay acefay.
Eakspay otnay, eplyray otnay, oday otnay answeray emay.
Ymay ingersfay itchay. Ifeway, eway arcescay oughtthay usay estblay
Atthay Odgay adhay entlay usay utbay isthay onlyay ildchay;
Utbay ownay Iay eesay isthay oneay isay oneay ootay uchmay,
Anday atthay eway avehay aay ursecay inay avinghay erhay.
Outay onay erhay, ildinghay.

URSENay.
Odgay inay eavenhay essblay erhay.
Youay areay otay ameblay, ymay ordlay, otay ateray erhay osay.

APULETCay.
Anday ywhay, ymay adylay isdomway? Oldhay youray onguetay,
Oodgay udencepray; attersmay ithway youray ossipsgay, ogay.

URSENay.
Iay eakspay onay easontray.

APULETCay.
Oay Odgay yeay ood-engay!

URSENay.
Aymay otnay oneay eakspay?

APULETCay.
Eacepay, youay umblingmay oolfay!
Utteray youray avitygray o’eray aay ossip’sgay owlbay,
Orfay erehay eway eednay itay otnay.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Youay areay ootay othay.

APULETCay.
Od’sgay eadbray, itay akesmay emay admay!
Ayday, ightnay, ourhay, ideray, imetay, orkway, ayplay,
Aloneay, inay ompanycay, illstay ymay arecay athhay eenbay
Otay avehay erhay atch’dmay, anday avinghay ownay ovidedpray
Aay entlemangay ofay oblenay arentagepay,
Ofay airfay emesnesday, youthfulay, anday oblynay allieday,
Uff’dstay, asay eythay aysay, ithway onourablehay artspay,
Oportion’dpray asay one’say oughtthay ouldway ishway aay anmay,
Anday enthay otay avehay aay etchedwray ulingpay oolfay,
Aay iningwhay ammetmay, inay erhay ortune’sfay endertay,
Otay answeray, I’ll‘ay otnay edway, Iay annotcay ovelay,
Iay amay ootay youngay, Iay aypray youay ardonpay emay.’
Utbay, anday youay illway otnay edway, I’llay ardonpay youay.
Azegray erewhay youay illway, youay allshay otnay ousehay ithway emay.
Ooklay o’ttay, inkthay on’tay, Iay oday otnay useay otay estjay.
Ursdaythay isay earnay; aylay andhay onay earthay, adviseay.
Anday youay ebay inemay, I’llay ivegay youay otay ymay iendfray;
Anday youay ebay otnay, anghay, egbay, arvestay, ieday inay ethay eetsstray,
Orfay ybay ymay oulsay, I’llay e’ernay acknowledgeay eethay,
Ornay atwhay isay inemay allshay evernay oday eethay oodgay.
Usttray o’ttay, ethinkbay youay, I’llay otnay ebay orswornfay.

 Exit[_ay._]

ULIETJay.
Isay erethay onay itypay ittingsay inay ethay oudsclay,
Atthay eessay intoay ethay ottombay ofay ymay iefgray?
Oay eetsway ymay othermay, astcay emay otnay awayay,
Elayday isthay arriagemay orfay aay onthmay, aay eekway,
Oray, ifay youay oday otnay, akemay ethay idalbray edbay
Inay atthay imday onumentmay erewhay Ybalttay ieslay.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Alktay otnay otay emay, orfay I’llay otnay eakspay aay ordway.
Oday asay outhay iltway, orfay Iay avehay oneday ithway eethay.

 Exit[_ay._]

ULIETJay.
Oay Odgay! Oay Ursenay, owhay allshay isthay ebay eventedpray?
Ymay usbandhay isay onay earthay, ymay aithfay inay eavenhay.
Owhay allshay atthay aithfay eturnray againay otay earthay,
Unlessay atthay usbandhay endsay itay emay omfray eavenhay
Ybay eavinglay earthay? Omfortcay emay, ounselcay emay.
Alackay, alackay, atthay eavenhay ouldshay actisepray atagemsstray
Uponay osay oftsay aay ubjectsay asay yselfmay.
Atwhay ay’stsay outhay? Asthay outhay otnay aay ordway ofay oyjay?
Omesay omfortcay, Ursenay.

URSENay.
Aithfay, erehay itay isay.
Omeoray isay anishedbay; anday allay ethay orldway otay othingnay
Atthay ehay aresday e’ernay omecay ackbay otay allengechay youay.
Oray ifay ehay oday, itay eedsnay ustmay ebay ybay ealthstay.
Enthay, incesay ethay asecay osay andsstay asay ownay itay othday,
Iay inkthay itay estbay youay arriedmay ithway ethay Ountycay.
Oay, e’shay aay ovelylay entlemangay.
Omeo’sray aay ishcloutday otay imhay. Anay eagleay, adammay,
Athhay otnay osay eengray, osay uickqay, osay airfay anay eyeay
Asay Arispay athhay. Eshrewbay ymay eryvay earthay,
Iay inkthay youay areay appyhay inay isthay econdsay atchmay,
Orfay itay excelsay youray irstfay: oray ifay itay idday otnay,
Youray irstfay isay eadday, oray ere’tway asay oodgay ehay ereway,
Asay ivinglay erehay anday youay onay useay ofay imhay.

ULIETJay.
Eakestspay outhay omfray ythay earthay?

URSENay.
Anday omfray ymay oulsay ootay,
Oray elseay eshrewbay emthay othbay.

ULIETJay.
Amenay.

URSENay.
Atwhay?

ULIETJay.
Ellway, outhay asthay omfortedcay emay arvellousmay uchmay.
Ogay inay, anday elltay ymay adylay Iay amay onegay,
Avinghay ispleas’dday ymay atherfay, otay Awrencelay’ ellcay,
Otay akemay onfessioncay anday otay ebay absolv’day.

URSENay.
Arrymay, Iay illway; anday isthay isay iselyway oneday.

 Exit[_ay._]

ULIETJay.
Ancientay amnationday! Oay ostmay ickedway iendfay!
Isay itay oremay insay otay ishway emay usthay orswornfay,
Oray otay ispraiseday ymay ordlay ithway atthay amesay onguetay
Ichwhay eshay athhay ais’dpray imhay ithway aboveay omparecay
Osay anymay ousandthay imestay? Ogay, ounsellorcay.
Outhay anday ymay osombay enceforthhay allshay ebay aintway.
I’llay otay ethay Iarfray otay owknay ishay emedyray.
Ifay allay elseay ailfay, yselfmay avehay owerpay otay ieday.

 Exit[_ay._]




ACTay IVay

ENESCay Iay. Iarfray Awrence’slay Ellcay.


 Enteray Iarfray Awrencelay anday Arispay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Onay Ursdaythay, irsay? Ethay imetay isay eryvay ortshay.

ARISPay.
Ymay atherfay Apuletcay illway avehay itay osay;
Anday Iay amay othingnay owslay otay ackslay ishay astehay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Youay aysay youay oday otnay owknay ethay ady’slay indmay.
Unevenay isay ethay oursecay; Iay ikelay itay otnay.

ARISPay.
Immoderatelyay eshay eepsway orfay Ybalt’stay eathday,
Anday ereforethay avehay Iay ittlelay alk’dtay ofay ovelay;
Orfay Enusvay ilessmay otnay inay aay ousehay ofay earstay.
Ownay, irsay, erhay atherfay ountscay itay angerousday
Atthay eshay oday ivegay erhay orrowsay osay uchmay aysway;
Anday inay ishay isdomway, asteshay ouray arriagemay,
Otay opstay ethay inundationay ofay erhay earstay,
Ichwhay, ootay uchmay indedmay ybay erselfhay aloneay,
Aymay ebay utpay omfray erhay ybay ocietysay.
Ownay oday youay owknay ethay easonray ofay isthay astehay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Aside[_ay._] Iay ouldway Iay ewknay otnay ywhay itay ouldshay ebay ow’dslay.—
Ooklay, irsay, erehay omescay ethay adylay owardtay ymay ellcay.

 Enteray Ulietjay.

ARISPay.
Appilyhay etmay, ymay adylay anday ymay ifeway!

ULIETJay.
Atthay aymay ebay, irsay, enwhay Iay aymay ebay aay ifeway.

ARISPay.
Atthay aymay ebay, ustmay ebay, ovelay, onay Ursdaythay extnay.

ULIETJay.
Atwhay ustmay ebay allshay ebay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
At’sthay aay ertaincay exttay.

ARISPay.
Omecay youay otay akemay onfessioncay otay isthay atherfay?

ULIETJay.
Otay answeray atthay, Iay ouldshay onfesscay otay youay.

ARISPay.
Oday otnay enyday otay imhay atthay youay ovelay emay.

ULIETJay.
Iay illway onfesscay otay youay atthay Iay ovelay imhay.

ARISPay.
Osay illway yeay, Iay amay uresay, atthay youay ovelay emay.

ULIETJay.
Ifay Iay oday osay, itay illway ebay ofay oremay icepray,
Eingbay okespay ehindbay youray ackbay anthay otay youray acefay.

ARISPay.
Oorpay oulsay, ythay acefay isay uchmay abus’day ithway earstay.

ULIETJay.
Ethay earstay avehay otgay allsmay ictoryvay ybay atthay;
Orfay itay asway adbay enoughay eforebay eirthay itespay.

ARISPay.
Outhay ong’stwray itay oremay anthay earstay ithway atthay eportray.

ULIETJay.
Atthay isay onay anderslay, irsay, ichwhay isay aay uthtray,
Anday atwhay Iay akespay, Iay akespay itay otay ymay acefay.

ARISPay.
Ythay acefay isay inemay, anday outhay asthay ander’dslay itay.

ULIETJay.
Itay aymay ebay osay, orfay itay isay otnay inemay ownay.
Areay youay atay eisurelay, olyhay atherfay, ownay,
Oray allshay Iay omecay otay youay atay eveningay assmay?

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Ymay eisurelay ervessay emay, ensivepay aughterday, ownay.—
Ymay ordlay, eway ustmay entreatay ethay imetay aloneay.

ARISPay.
Odgay ieldshay Iay ouldshay isturbday evotionday!—
Ulietjay, onay Ursdaythay earlyay illway Iay ouseray yeay,
Illtay enthay, adieuay; anday eepkay isthay olyhay isskay.

 Exit[_ay._]

ULIETJay.
Oay utshay ethay oorday, anday enwhay outhay asthay oneday osay,
Omecay eepway ithway emay, astpay opehay, astpay urecay, astpay elphay!

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Oay Ulietjay, Iay alreadyay owknay ythay iefgray;
Itay ainsstray emay astpay ethay ompasscay ofay ymay itsway.
Iay earhay outhay ustmay, anday othingnay aymay oroguepray itay,
Onay Ursdaythay extnay ebay arriedmay otay isthay Ountycay.

ULIETJay.
Elltay emay otnay, Iarfray, atthay outhay ear’sthay ofay isthay,
Unlessay outhay elltay emay owhay Iay aymay eventpray itay.
Ifay inay ythay isdomway, outhay anstcay ivegay onay elphay,
Oday outhay utbay allcay ymay esolutionray iseway,
Anday ithway isthay ifeknay I’llay elphay itay esentlypray.
Odgay oin’djay ymay earthay anday Omeo’sray, outhay ouray andshay;
Anday ereay isthay andhay, ybay eethay otay Omeo’sray eal’dsay,
Allshay ebay ethay abellay otay anotheray eedday,
Oray ymay uetray earthay ithway eacheroustray evoltray
Urntay otay anotheray, isthay allshay ayslay emthay othbay.
Ereforethay, outay ofay ythay ong-experienc’dlay imetay,
Ivegay emay omesay esentpray ounselcay, oray eholdbay
Ixt’tway ymay extremesay anday emay isthay oodyblay ifeknay
Allshay ayplay ethay empireay, arbitratingay atthay
Ichwhay ethay ommissioncay ofay ythay yearsay anday artay
Ouldcay otay onay issueay ofay uetray onourhay ingbray.
Ebay otnay osay onglay otay eakspay. Iay onglay otay ieday,
Ifay atwhay outhay eak’stspay eakspay otnay ofay emedyray.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Oldhay, aughterday. Iay oday yspay aay indkay ofay opehay,
Ichwhay avescray asay esperateday anay executionay
Asay atthay isay esperateday ichwhay eway ouldway eventpray.
Ifay, atherray anthay otay arrymay Ountycay Arispay
Outhay asthay ethay engthstray ofay illway otay ayslay yselfthay,
Enthay isay itay ikelylay outhay iltway undertakeay
Aay ingthay ikelay eathday otay idechay awayay isthay ameshay,
Atthay op’stcay ithway eathday imselfhay otay apescay omfray itay.
Anday ifay outhay ar’stday, I’llay ivegay eethay emedyray.

ULIETJay.
Oay, idbay emay eaplay, atherray anthay arrymay Arispay,
Omfray offay ethay attlementsbay ofay yonderay owertay,
Oray alkway inay ievishthay aysway, oray idbay emay urklay
Erewhay erpentssay areay. Ainchay emay ithway oaringray earsbay;
Oray idehay emay ightlynay inay aay arnel-housechay,
O’er-cover’day uiteqay ithway eadday en’smay attlingray onesbay,
Ithway eekyray anksshay anday yelloway aplesschay ullsskay.
Oray idbay emay ogay intoay aay ew-madenay avegray,
Anday idehay emay ithway aay eadday anmay inay ishay oudshray;
Ingsthay atthay, otay earhay emthay oldtay, avehay ademay emay embletray,
Anday Iay illway oday itay ithoutway earfay oray oubtday,
Otay ivelay anay unstain’day ifeway otay ymay eetsway ovelay.

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Oldhay enthay. Ogay omehay, ebay errymay, ivegay onsentcay
Otay arrymay Arispay. Ednesdayway isay omorrowtay;
Omorrowtay ightnay ooklay atthay outhay ielay aloneay,
Etlay otnay ythay Ursenay ielay ithway eethay inay ythay amberchay.
Aketay outhay isthay ialvay, eingbay enthay inay edbay,
Anday isthay istilledday iquorlay inkdray outhay offay,
Enwhay esentlypray oughthray allay ythay einsvay allshay unray
Aay oldcay anday owsydray umourhay; orfay onay ulsepay
Allshay eepkay ishay ativenay ogresspray, utbay urceasesay.
Onay armthway, onay eathbray allshay estifytay outhay ivestlay,
Ethay osesray inay ythay ipslay anday eekschay allshay adefay
Otay alypay ashesay; ythay eyesay’ indowsway allfay,
Ikelay eathday enwhay ehay utsshay upay ethay ayday ofay ifelay.
Eachay artpay epriv’dday ofay upplesay overnmentgay,
Allshay iffstay anday arkstay anday oldcay appearay ikelay eathday.
Anday inay isthay orrow’dbay ikenesslay ofay unkshray eathday
Outhay altshay ontinuecay otway anday ortyfay ourshay,
Anday enthay awakeay asay omfray aay easantplay eepslay.
Ownay enwhay ethay idegroombray inay ethay orningmay omescay
Otay ouseray eethay omfray ythay edbay, erethay artay outhay eadday.
Enthay asay ethay annermay ofay ouray ountrycay isay,
Inay ythay estbay obesray, uncover’day, onay ethay ierbay,
Outhay altshay ebay ornebay otay atthay amesay ancientay aultvay
Erewhay allay ethay indredkay ofay ethay Apuletscay ielay.
Inay ethay eantimemay, againstay outhay altshay awakeay,
Allshay Omeoray ybay ymay etterslay owknay ouray iftdray,
Anday itherhay allshay ehay omecay, anday ehay anday Iay
Illway atchway ythay akingway, anday atthay eryvay ightnay
Allshay Omeoray earbay eethay encehay otay Antuamay.
Anday isthay allshay eefray eethay omfray isthay esentpray ameshay,
Ifay onay inconstantay oytay ornay omanishway earfay
Abateay ythay alourvay inay ethay actingay itay.

ULIETJay.
Ivegay emay, ivegay emay! Oay elltay otnay emay ofay earfay!

IARFRay AWRENCELay.
Oldhay; etgay youay onegay, ebay ongstray anday osperouspray
Inay isthay esolveray. I’llay endsay aay iarfray ithway eedspay
Otay Antuamay, ithway ymay etterslay otay ythay ordlay.

ULIETJay.
Ovelay ivegay emay engthstray, anday engthstray allshay elphay afforday.
Arewellfay, earday atherfay.

 Exeunt[_ay._]

ENESCay IIay. Allhay inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.

 Enteray Apuletcay, Adylay Apuletcay, Ursenay anday Ervantssay.

APULETCay.
Osay anymay uestsgay inviteay asay erehay areay itwray.

 Exit[_ay irstfay Ervantsay._]

Irrahsay, ogay irehay emay entytway unningcay ookscay.

ECONDSay ERVANTSay.
Youay allshay avehay onenay illay, irsay; orfay I’llay ytray ifay eythay ancay icklay eirthay
ingersfay.

APULETCay.
Owhay anstcay outhay ytray emthay osay?

ECONDSay ERVANTSay.
Arrymay, irsay, is’tay anay illay ookcay atthay annotcay icklay ishay ownay ingersfay;
ereforethay ehay atthay annotcay icklay ishay ingersfay oesgay otnay ithway emay.

APULETCay.
Ogay, egonebay.

 Exit[_ay econdsay Ervantsay._]

Eway allshay ebay uchmay unfurnish’day orfay isthay imetay.
Atwhay, isay ymay aughterday onegay otay Iarfray Awrencelay?

URSENay.
Ayay, orsoothfay.

APULETCay.
Ellway, ehay aymay ancechay otay oday omesay oodgay onay erhay.
Aay eevishpay elf-will’dsay arlotryhay itay isay.

 Enteray Ulietjay.

URSENay.
Eesay erewhay eshay omescay omfray iftshray ithway errymay ooklay.

APULETCay.
Owhay ownay, ymay eadstronghay. Erewhay avehay youay eenbay addinggay?

ULIETJay.
Erewhay Iay avehay earntlay emay otay epentray ethay insay
Ofay isobedientday oppositionay
Otay youay anday youray ehestsbay; anday amay enjoin’day
Ybay olyhay Awrencelay otay allfay ostratepray erehay,
Otay egbay youray ardonpay. Ardonpay, Iay eseechbay youay.
Enceforwardhay Iay amay everay ul’dray ybay youay.

APULETCay.
Endsay orfay ethay Ountycay, ogay elltay imhay ofay isthay.
I’llay avehay isthay otknay itknay upay omorrowtay orningmay.

ULIETJay.
Iay etmay ethay youthfulay ordlay atay Awrencelay’ ellcay,
Anday avegay imhay atwhay ecomedbay ovelay Iay ightmay,
Otnay eppingstay o’eray ethay oundsbay ofay odestymay.

APULETCay.
Ywhay, Iay amay adglay on’tay. Isthay isay ellway. Andstay upay.
Isthay isay as’tay ouldshay ebay. Etlay emay eesay ethay Ountycay.
Ayay, arrymay. Ogay, Iay aysay, anday etchfay imhay itherhay.
Ownay aforeay Odgay, isthay everendray olyhay Iarfray,
Allay ouray olewhay itycay isay uchmay oundbay otay imhay.

ULIETJay.
Ursenay, illway youay ogay ithway emay intoay ymay osetclay,
Otay elphay emay ortsay uchsay eedfulnay ornamentsay
Asay youay inkthay itfay otay urnishfay emay omorrowtay?

ADYLay APULETCay.
Onay, otnay illtay Ursdaythay. Erethay isay imetay enoughay.

APULETCay.
Ogay, Ursenay, ogay ithway erhay. E’llway otay urchchay omorrowtay.

 Exeunt[_ay Ulietjay anday Ursenay._]

ADYLay APULETCay.
Eway allshay ebay ortshay inay ouray ovisionpray,
Is’tay ownay earnay ightnay.

APULETCay.
Ushtay, Iay illway irstay aboutay,
Anday allay ingsthay allshay ebay ellway, Iay arrantway eethay, ifeway.
Ogay outhay otay Ulietjay, elphay otay eckday upay erhay.
I’llay otnay otay edbay onighttay, etlay emay aloneay.
I’llay ayplay ethay ousewifehay orfay isthay once.—Whatay, ohay!—
Eythay areay allay orthfay: ellway, Iay illway alkway yselfmay
Otay Ountycay Arispay, otay eparepray imhay upay
Againstay omorrowtay. Ymay earthay isay ondrousway ightlay
Incesay isthay amesay aywardway irlgay isay osay eclaim’dray.

 Exeunt[_ay._]

ENESCay IIIay. Uliet’sjay Amberchay.

 Enteray Ulietjay anday Ursenay.

ULIETJay.
Ayay, osethay attiresay areay estbay. Utbay, entlegay Ursenay,
Iay aypray eethay eavelay emay otay yselfmay onighttay;
Orfay Iay avehay eednay ofay anymay orisonsay
Otay ovemay ethay eavenshay otay ilesmay uponay ymay atestay,
Ichwhay, ellway outhay ow’stknay, isay osscray anday ullfay ofay insay.

 Enteray Adylay Apuletcay.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Atwhay, areay youay usybay, ohay? Eednay youay ymay elphay?

ULIETJay.
Onay, adammay; eway avehay ull’dcay uchsay ecessariesnay
Asay areay ehovefulbay orfay ouray atestay omorrowtay.
Osay easeplay youay, etlay emay ownay ebay eftlay aloneay,
Anday etlay ethay ursenay isthay ightnay itsay upay ithway youay,
Orfay Iay amay uresay youay avehay youray andshay ullfay allay
Inay isthay osay uddensay usinessbay.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Oodgay ightnay.
Etgay eethay otay edbay anday estray, orfay outhay asthay eednay.

 Exeunt[_ay Adylay Apuletcay anday Ursenay._]

ULIETJay.
Arewellfay. Odgay owsknay enwhay eway allshay eetmay againay.
Iay avehay aay aintfay oldcay earfay illsthray oughthray ymay einsvay
Atthay almostay eezesfray upay ethay eathay ofay ifelay.
I’llay allcay emthay ackbay againay otay omfortcay emay.
Urse!—Whatnay ouldshay eshay oday erehay?
Ymay ismalday enescay Iay eedsnay ustmay actay aloneay.
Omecay, ialvay.
Atwhay ifay isthay ixturemay oday otnay orkway atay allay?
Allshay Iay ebay arriedmay enthay omorrowtay orningmay?
Onay, Onay! Isthay allshay orbidfay itay. Ielay outhay erethay.

 Aying[_lay ownday erhay aggerday._]

Atwhay ifay itay ebay aay oisonpay, ichwhay ethay Iarfray
Ubtlysay athhay inister’dmay otay avehay emay eadday,
Estlay inay isthay arriagemay ehay ouldshay ebay ishonour’dday,
Ecausebay ehay arriedmay emay eforebay otay Omeoray?
Iay earfay itay isay. Anday yetay ethinksmay itay ouldshay otnay,
Orfay ehay athhay illstay eenbay iedtray aay olyhay anmay.
Owhay ifay, enwhay Iay amay aidlay intoay ethay ombtay,
Iay akeway eforebay ethay imetay atthay Omeoray
Omecay otay edeemray emay? Ere’sthay aay earfulfay ointpay!
Allshay Iay otnay enthay ebay ifledstay inay ethay aultvay,
Otay osewhay oulfay outhmay onay ealthsomehay airay eathesbray inay,
Anday erethay ieday angledstray ereay ymay Omeoray omescay?
Oray, ifay Iay ivelay, isay itay otnay eryvay ikelay,
Ethay orriblehay onceitcay ofay eathday anday ightnay,
Ogethertay ithway ethay errortay ofay ethay aceplay,
Asay inay aay aultvay, anay ancientay eceptacleray,
Erewhay orfay isthay anymay undredhay yearsay ethay onesbay
Ofay allay ymay uriedbay ancestorsay areay ack’dpay,
Erewhay oodyblay Ybalttay, yetay utbay eengray inay earthay,
Ieslay esteringfay inay ishay oudshray; erewhay, asay eythay aysay,
Atay omesay ourshay inay ethay ightnay iritsspay esortray—
Alackay, alackay, isay itay otnay ikelay atthay Iay,
Osay earlyay akingway, atwhay ithway oathsomelay ellssmay,
Anday ieksshray ikelay andrakesmay orntay outay ofay ethay earthay,
Atthay ivinglay ortalsmay, earinghay emthay, unray admay.
Oay, ifay Iay akeway, allshay Iay otnay ebay istraughtday,
Environeday ithway allay esethay ideoushay earsfay,
Anday adlymay ayplay ithway ymay orefathersfay’ ointsjay?
Anday uckplay ethay angledmay Ybalttay omfray ishay oudshray?
Anday, inay isthay ageray, ithway omesay eatgray insman’skay onebay,
Asay ithway aay ubclay, ashday outay ymay esperateday ainsbray?
Oay ooklay, ethinksmay Iay eesay ymay ousin’scay ostghay
Eekingsay outay Omeoray atthay idday itspay ishay odybay
Uponay aay apier’sray ointpay. Aystay, Ybalttay, aystay!
Omeoray, Omeoray, Omeoray, ere’shay inkdray! Iay inkdray otay eethay.

 Ows[_thray erselfhay onay ethay edbay._]

ENESCay IVay. Allhay inay Apulet’scay Ousehay.

 Enteray Adylay Apuletcay anday Ursenay.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Oldhay, aketay esethay eyskay anday etchfay oremay icesspay, Ursenay.

URSENay.
Eythay allcay orfay atesday anday uincesqay inay ethay astrypay.

 Enteray Apuletcay.

APULETCay.
Omecay, irstay, irstay, irstay! Ethay econdsay ockcay athhay ow’dcray,
Ethay urfewcay ellbay athhay ungray, is’tay eethray o’clockay.
Ooklay otay ethay ak’dbay eatsmay, oodgay Angelicaay;
Arespay otnay orfay ostcay.

URSENay.
Ogay, youay ot-queancay, ogay,
Etgay youay otay edbay; aithfay, you’llay ebay icksay omorrowtay
Orfay isthay ight’snay atchingway.

APULETCay.
Onay, otnay aay itwhay. Atwhay! Iay avehay atch’dway ereay ownay
Allay ightnay orfay esserlay ausecay, anday e’ernay eenbay icksay.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Ayay, youay avehay eenbay aay ouse-huntmay inay youray imetay;
Utbay Iay illway atchway youay omfray uchsay atchingway ownay.

 Exeunt[_ay Adylay Apuletcay anday Ursenay._]

APULETCay.
Aay ealous-hoodjay, aay ealous-hoodjay!

 Enteray Ervantssay, ithway itsspay, ogslay anday asketsbay.

Ownay, ellowfay, at’swhay erethay?

IRSTFay ERVANTSay.
Ingsthay orfay ethay ookcay, irsay; utbay Iay owknay otnay atwhay.

APULETCay.
Akemay astehay, akemay astehay.

 Exit[_ay Irstfay Ervantsay._]

Irrah—say, etchfay ierdray ogslay.
Allcay Eterpay, ehay illway owshay eethay erewhay eythay areay.

ECONDSay ERVANTSay.
Iay avehay aay eadhay, irsay, atthay illway indfay outay ogslay
Anday evernay oubletray Eterpay orfay ethay attermay.

 Exit[_ay._]

APULETCay.
Assmay anday ellway aidsay; aay errymay oresonwhay, ahay.
Outhay altshay ebay Oggerhead.—Goodlay aithfay, is’tay ayday.
Ethay Ountycay illway ebay erehay ithway usicmay aightstray,
Orfay osay ehay aidsay ehay ouldway. Iay earhay imhay earnay.

 Ay[_play usicmay._]

Ursenay! Ifeway! Atwhay, ohay! Atwhay, Ursenay, Iay aysay!

 E-enterray Ursenay.

Ogay akenway Ulietjay, ogay anday imtray erhay upay.
I’llay ogay anday atchay ithway Arispay. Iehay, akemay astehay,
Akemay astehay; ethay idegroombray ehay isay omecay alreadyay.
Akemay astehay Iay aysay.

 Exeunt[_ay._]

ENESCay Vay. Uliet’sjay Amberchay; Ulietjay onay ethay edbay.

 Enteray Ursenay.

URSENay.
Istressmay! Atwhay, istressmay! Ulietjay! Astfay, Iay arrantway erhay, eshay.
Ywhay, amblay, ywhay, adylay, iefay, youay ug-abedslay!
Ywhay, ovelay, Iay aysay! Adammay! Eetheartsway! Ywhay, idebray!
Atwhay, otnay aay ordway? Youay aketay youray ennyworthspay ownay.
Eepslay orfay aay eekway; orfay ethay extnay ightnay, Iay arrantway,
Ethay Ountycay Arispay athhay etsay upay ishay estray
Atthay youay allshay estray utbay ittlelay. Odgay orgivefay emay!
Arrymay anday amenay. Owhay oundsay isay eshay asleepay!
Iay eedsnay ustmay akeway erhay. Adammay, adammay, adammay!
Ayay, etlay ethay Ountycay aketay youay inay youray edbay,
E’llhay ightfray youay upay, i’faithay. Illway itay otnay ebay?
Atwhay, ess’ddray, anday inay youray othesclay, anday ownday againay?
Iay ustmay eedsnay akeway youay. Adylay! Adylay! Adylay!
Alasay, alasay! Elphay, elphay! Ymay ady’slay eadday!
Oay, ell-a-dayway atthay everay Iay asway ornbay.
Omesay aquaay itaevay, ohay! Ymay ordlay! Ymay adylay!

 Enteray Adylay Apuletcay.

ADYLay APULETCay.
Atwhay oisenay isay erehay?

URSENay.
Oay amentablelay ayday!

ADYLay APULETCay.
Atwhay isay ethay attermay?

URSENay.
Ooklay, ooklay! Oay eavyhay ayday!

ADYLay APULETCay.
Oay emay, Oay emay! Ymay ildchay, ymay onlyay ifelay.
Eviveray, ooklay upay, oray Iay illway ieday ithway eethay.
Elphay, elphay! Allcay elphay.

 Enteray Apuletcay.

APULETCay.
Orfay ameshay, ingbray Ulietjay orthfay, erhay ordlay isay omecay.

URSENay.
E’sshay eadday, eceas’dday, e’sshay eadday; alackay ethay ayday!

ADYLay APULETCay.
Alackay ethay ayday, e’sshay eadday, e’sshay eadday, e’sshay eadday!

APULETCay.
Ahay! Etlay emay eesay erhay. Outay alasay! E’sshay oldcay,
Erhay oodblay isay ettledsay anday erhay ointsjay areay iffstay.
Ifelay anday esethay ipslay avehay onglay eenbay eparatedsay.
Eathday ieslay onay erhay ikelay anay untimelyay ostfray
Uponay ethay eetestsway owerflay ofay allay ethay ieldfay.

URSENay.
